In " Roza și ceilalți " , the libertine daughter of a Jewish tailor is persuaded by her coreligionists into accepting the sexual advances of a Nazi German officer . ||| En " Roza și ceilalți ", la hija libertina de un sastre judío es persuadida por sus correligionistas de aceptar los avances sexuales de un oficial alemán nazi.
Her mother , Josephine Marie Ranch , was a tailor , and her father , Ernest Norman , a carpenter . ||| Su madre, Josephine Marie Ranch, era una sastre, y su padre, Ernest Norman, un carpintero.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a housewife . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.
Her father was a tailor and soon after her birth , the family moved to Princes Town , where Cadogan grew up and attended the Government Primary School . ||| Su padre era un sastre y poco después de su nacimiento, la familia se trasladó a Princes Town, donde Cadogan creció y asistió a la Escuela Primaria del Gobierno.
Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija de inmigrantes catalanes - judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.
Gloria grew up in a low - income household in the suburbs of Rio de Janeiro , with her father working as a tailor and her mother , a housewife . ||| Gloria creció en un hogar de bajos ingresos en los suburbios de Río de Janeiro, con su padre trabajando como sastre y su madre, ama de casa.
Her father was Richard Dean Tucker who was a tailor and her mother was Amelia Tucker . ||| Su padre era Richard Dean Tucker que era un sastre y su madre era Amelia Tucker.
Little is known about Sara Jeffrey besides that Paul Jeffrey , her father , was a tailor and her mother was Ellen , who lived with the Miltons until her death in 1611 . ||| Poco se sabe de Sara Jeffrey además de que Paul Jeffrey, su padre, era un sastre y su madre era Ellen, que vivió con los Miltons hasta su muerte en 1611.
Over the course of hundreds of hours the mistress tailor filmed herself while making a three - piece suit . ||| En el transcurso de cientos de horas la sastre se filmó a sí misma mientras hacía un traje de tres piezas.

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.
The President was a former tailor himself , and often preferred to sew his buttons on personally . ||| El Presidente era un antiguo sastre, y a menudo prefería coser sus botones personalmente.
The tailor stuck his legs out the window and threatened the bear with the claim that they were a vise . ||| El sastre metió sus piernas por la ventana y amenazó al oso con la afirmación de que eran una visera.
His tailor is late making his suit ; with the dance well underway , it is barely being held together by basting stitches , but Harold puts it on and hopes for the best . ||| Su sastre es tarde haciendo su traje; con el baile bien en marcha, apenas se mantiene unido por puntos de batir, pero Harold se lo pone y espera lo mejor.
On June 10 , 1737 , the day after Pentecost , at three in the afternoon , " lightning struck the chapel , in front of the altar , hitting a Papist German tailor and his wife , who had taken shelter there ... ||| El 10 de junio de 1737, el día después de Pentecostés, a las tres de la tarde, " un rayo golpeó la capilla, frente al altar, golpeando a un sastre papista alemán y su esposa, que había tomado refugio allí...
Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.
Dai excels in many things , including being a skilled tailor himself . ||| Dai sobresale en muchas cosas, incluyendo ser un sastre experto en sí mismo.
The son of a Spanish tailor , he dedicated himself to the same profession , and was first elected as a union delegate of the tailors in 1938 . ||| El hijo de un sastre español, se dedicó a la misma profesión, y fue elegido por primera vez como delegado sindical de los sastres en 1938.
Nearby in the same village , a young peasant tailor ( Mickey Mouse ) kills seven flies at once while at his work , and accidentally interjects several other peasants ' discussion of the problems with the giant to brag loudly about his accomplishment : ||| Cerca en el mismo pueblo, un joven sastre campesino ( Mickey Mouse ) mata siete moscas a la vez mientras que en su trabajo, y accidentalmente interpone varios otros campesinos'discusión de los problemas con el gigante para presumir en voz alta sobre su logro :
Within the next year , a local tailor cured his leprosy by washing in the same spring . ||| Dentro del año siguiente, un sastre local curó su lepra lavándose en la misma primavera.

After he married on 13 October 1854 he commenced business as a tailor himself in Llanrwst , and remained there for the rest of his life . ||| Después de casarse el 13 de octubre de 1854 comenzó a trabajar como sastre en Llanrwst, y permaneció allí por el resto de su vida.
Leszek Miller was born in Żyrardów , Miller comes from a poor , working - class family : His father was a tailor and his mother a needlewoman . ||| Leszek Miller nació en Ayrardów, Miller proviene de una familia pobre de clase trabajadora : Su padre era un sastre y su madre una mujer aguja.
His father was a native of Alsace who worked as a tailor and his mother was from East Frisia in Germany . ||| Su padre era un nativo de Alsacia que trabajaba como sastre y su madre era de Frisia Oriental en Alemania.
She was born in Bodø as a daughter of tailor , editor and missionary Jakob Andreas Hanssen and his wife Mathilde Dahl . ||| Nació en Bodø como hija del sastre, editor y misionero Jakob Andreas Hanssen y su esposa Mathilde Dahl.
A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.
" The Big Winner " about a poor tailor and his winning lottery ticket . ||| "El Gran Ganador" sobre un pobre sastre y su boleto de lotería ganador.
By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".
A tailor by trade , he opened his own clothing store in 1913 . ||| Un sastre por el comercio, abrió su propia tienda de ropa en 1913.

The tailor stuck his legs out the window and threatened the bear with the claim that they were a vise . ||| El sastre metió sus piernas por la ventana y amenazó al oso con la afirmación de que eran una visera.
His tailor is late making his suit ; with the dance well underway , it is barely being held together by basting stitches , but Harold puts it on and hopes for the best . ||| Su sastre es tarde haciendo su traje; con el baile bien en marcha, apenas se está sosteniendo juntos por basting puntos, pero Harold se lo pone y espera lo mejor.
On June 10 , 1737 , the day after Pentecost , at three in the afternoon , " lightning struck the chapel , in front of the altar , hitting a Papist German tailor and his wife , who had taken shelter there ... ||| El 10 de junio de 1737, el día después de Pentecostés, a las tres de la tarde, " un rayo golpeó la capilla, delante del altar, golpeando a un sastre papista alemán y su esposa, que se había refugiado allí...
Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia ( Croacia actual - día ), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910 ; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.
Dai excels in many things , including being a skilled tailor himself . ||| Dai sobresale en muchas cosas, incluyendo ser un sastre experto.
The son of a Spanish tailor , he dedicated himself to the same profession , and was first elected as a union delegate of the tailors in 1938 . ||| Hijo de un sastre español, se dedicó a la misma profesión, y fue elegido por primera vez como delegado sindical de los sastres en 1938.
Nearby in the same village , a young peasant tailor ( Mickey Mouse ) kills seven flies at once while at his work , and accidentally interjects several other peasants ' discussion of the problems with the giant to brag loudly about his accomplishment : ||| Cerca de la misma aldea, un joven sastre campesino ( Mickey Mouse ) mata siete moscas a la vez mientras que en su trabajo, y accidentalmente interpone varios otros campesinos'discusión de los problemas con el gigante para presumir en voz alta sobre su logro :
Within the next year , a local tailor cured his leprosy by washing in the same spring . ||| Dentro del año siguiente, un sastre local curó su lepra lavándose en la misma primavera.

After he married on 13 October 1854 he commenced business as a tailor himself in Llanrwst , and remained there for the rest of his life . ||| Después de casarse el 13 de octubre de 1854 comenzó a trabajar como sastre en Llanrwst, y permaneció allí por el resto de su vida.

His father was a native of Alsace who worked as a tailor and his mother was from East Frisia in Germany . ||| Su padre era un nativo de Alsacia que trabajaba como sastre y su madre era de Frisia Oriental en Alemania.
She was born in Bodø as a daughter of tailor , editor and missionary Jakob Andreas Hanssen and his wife Mathilde Dahl . ||| Nació en Bodø como hija del sastre, editor y misionero Jakob Andreas Hanssen y su esposa Mathilde Dahl.
A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre en Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.
" The Big Winner " about a poor tailor and his winning lottery ticket . ||| "El Gran Ganador" sobre un pobre sastre y su boleto de lotería ganador.
By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".
A tailor by trade , he opened his own clothing store in 1913 . ||| Un sastre por oficio, abrió su propia tienda de ropa en 1913.

In " Roza și ceilalți " , the libertine daughter of a Jewish tailor is persuaded by her coreligionists into accepting the sexual advances of a Nazi German officer . ||| En " Roza și ceilalți ", la hija libertina de un sastre judío es persuadida por sus correligionistas de aceptar los avances sexuales de un oficial alemán nazi.

Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija de inmigrantes catalanes - judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era sastre y su madre ama de casa.

A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.
" The Big Winner " about a poor tailor and his winning lottery ticket . ||| "El Gran Ganador" sobre un pobre sastre y su boleto de lotería ganador.
By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia ( Croacia actual - día ), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910 ; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.

A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto; se especulaba que su legado se llevaba a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

She was born in Bodø as a daughter of tailor , editor and missionary Jakob Andreas Hanssen and his wife Mathilde Dahl . ||| Nació en Bodø como hija del sastre, editor y misionero Jakob Andreas Hanssen y su esposa Mathilde Dahl.
A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre en Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto; se especulaba que su legado se llevaba a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.
The President was a former tailor himself , and often preferred to sew his buttons on personally . ||| El Presidente era un antiguo sastre él mismo, y a menudo prefería coser sus botones personalmente.

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era conocido por su ingenio e intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

The son of a Spanish tailor , he dedicated himself to the same profession , and was first elected as a union delegate of the tailors in 1938 . ||| Hijo de un sastre español, se dedicó a la misma profesión, y fue elegido por primera vez como delegado sindical de los sastres en 1938.
Nearby in the same village , a young peasant tailor ( Mickey Mouse ) kills seven flies at once while at his work , and accidentally interjects several other peasants ' discussion of the problems with the giant to brag loudly about his accomplishment : ||| Cerca en el mismo pueblo, un joven sastre campesino ( Mickey Mouse ) mata siete moscas a la vez mientras que en su trabajo, e accidentalmente interpone varios otros campesinos'discusión de los problemas con el gigante para presumir en voz alta sobre su logro :

After he married on 13 October 1854 he commenced business as a tailor himself in Llanrwst , and remained there for the rest of his life . ||| Después de casarse el 13 de octubre de 1854 comenzó a trabajar como sastre en Llanrwst, y permaneció allí por el resto de su vida.

She was born in Bodø as a daughter of tailor , editor and missionary Jakob Andreas Hanssen and his wife Mathilde Dahl . ||| Nació en Bodø como hija del sastre, editor y misionero Jakob Andreas Hanssen y su esposa Mathilde Dahl.
A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.
" The Big Winner " about a poor tailor and his winning lottery ticket . ||| "El Gran Ganador" sobre un pobre sastre y su boleto de lotería ganador.
By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".
A tailor by trade , he opened his own clothing store in 1913 . ||| Un sastre de oficio, abrió su propia tienda de ropa en 1913.

Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija del catalán - inmigrantes judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era sastre y su madre ama de casa.

A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.
" The Big Winner " about a poor tailor and his winning lottery ticket . ||| "El gran ganador" sobre un pobre sastre y su boleto de lotería ganador.
By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".
A tailor by trade , he opened his own clothing store in 1913 . ||| Un sastre por oficio, abrió su propia tienda de ropa en 1913.

Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija de inmigrantes catalanes - judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.

Her mother , Josephine Marie Ranch , was a tailor , and her father , Ernest Norman , a carpenter . ||| Su madre, Josephine Marie Ranch, era una sastre, y su padre, Ernest Norman, un carpintero.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a housewife . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.
Her father was a tailor and soon after her birth , the family moved to Princes Town , where Cadogan grew up and attended the Government Primary School . ||| Su padre era sastre y poco después de su nacimiento, la familia se trasladó a Princes Town, donde Cadogan creció y asistió a la Escuela Primaria del Gobierno.
Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija de inmigrantes catalanes - judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.
Gloria grew up in a low - income household in the suburbs of Rio de Janeiro , with her father working as a tailor and her mother , a housewife . ||| Gloria creció en una casa de bajos ingresos en los suburbios de Río de Janeiro, con su padre trabajando como sastre y su madre, ama de casa.
Her father was Richard Dean Tucker who was a tailor and her mother was Amelia Tucker . ||| Su padre era Richard Dean Tucker que era un sastre y su madre era Amelia Tucker.
Little is known about Sara Jeffrey besides that Paul Jeffrey , her father , was a tailor and her mother was Ellen , who lived with the Miltons until her death in 1611 . ||| Poco se sabe de Sara Jeffrey además de que Paul Jeffrey, su padre, era un sastre y su madre era Ellen, que vivió con los Miltons hasta su muerte en 1611.

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.
The President was a former tailor himself , and often preferred to sew his buttons on personally . ||| El Presidente fue un antiguo sastre, y a menudo prefirió coser sus botones personalmente.
The tailor stuck his legs out the window and threatened the bear with the claim that they were a vise . ||| El sastre metió sus piernas por la ventana y amenazó al oso con la afirmación de que eran una visera.
His tailor is late making his suit ; with the dance well underway , it is barely being held together by basting stitches , but Harold puts it on and hopes for the best . ||| Su sastre es tarde haciendo su traje; con el baile bien en marcha, apenas se mantiene unido por puntos de batir, pero Harold se lo pone y espera lo mejor.

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.
Dai excels in many things , including being a skilled tailor himself . ||| Dai sobresale en muchas cosas, incluyendo ser un sastre experto.
The son of a Spanish tailor , he dedicated himself to the same profession , and was first elected as a union delegate of the tailors in 1938 . ||| Hijo de un sastre español, se dedicó a la misma profesión, y fue elegido por primera vez como delegado sindical de los sastres en 1938.

A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era conocido por su ingenio e intelecto; especulación si su legado se llevaba a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

A tailor in Gloucester sends his cat Simpkin to buy food and a twist of cherry - coloured silk to complete a waistcoat commissioned by the mayor for his wedding on Christmas morning . ||| Un sastre de Gloucester envía a su gato Simpkin a comprar comida y un toque de seda color cereza para completar un chaleco encargado por el alcalde para su boda en la mañana de Navidad.

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre " Pasquino " derivaba de un sastre cercano que era famoso por su ingenio e intelecto ; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a cabo a través de la estatua, en " el honor y el recuerdo eterno del pobre sastre ".
A tailor by trade , he opened his own clothing store in 1913 . ||| Un sastre por oficio, abrió su propia tienda de ropa en 1913.

In " Roza și ceilalți " , the libertine daughter of a Jewish tailor is persuaded by her coreligionists into accepting the sexual advances of a Nazi German officer . ||| En " Roza și ceilalți ", la hija libertina de un sastre judío es persuadida por sus correligionistas de aceptar los avances sexuales de un oficial alemán nazi.

Her father was a tailor and her mother a housewife . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.

Daughter of Catalan - Jewish immigrants who moved to Cuba , her father was a tailor and her mother was a seamstress . ||| Hija de inmigrantes catalanes - judíos que se mudaron a Cuba, su padre era sastre y su madre era costurera.
Her father was a tailor and her mother a homemaker . ||| Su padre era un sastre y su madre una ama de casa.

Little is known about Sara Jeffrey besides that Paul Jeffrey , her father , was a tailor and her mother was Ellen , who lived with the Miltons until her death in 1611 . ||| Poco se sabe de Sara Jeffrey además de que Paul Jeffrey, su padre, era un sastre y su madre era Ellen, que vivió con los Miltons hasta su muerte en 1611.

Diamond was born in Montreal , Quebec , Canada in 1920 to a tailor and his wife , but moved at a young age to Brooklyn , New York . ||| Diamond nació en Montreal, Quebec, Canadá en 1920 a un sastre y su esposa, pero se trasladó a una edad temprana a Brooklyn, Nueva York.

Born in Osijek , in the Austro - Hungarian Kingdom of Croatia - Slavonia ( present - day Croatia ) , he and his family moved to Zagreb in 1910 ; his father was a tailor and his mother a seamstress . ||| Nacido en Osijek, en el Reino Austro - Húngaro de Croacia - Eslavonia (actual - Croacia), él y su familia se trasladó a Zagreb en 1910; su padre era un sastre y su madre una costurera.
